                                   13419              .*  Queue a buffer in R4 onto the buffer chain before the pointer
                                   13420              .*    in R15.  The buffer chains are forward and backward chains to
                                   13421              .*    make it easy to add or delete members of the chain.
                                   13422              .*
                                   13423              &L       L     R0,PCBQB-PCB(,R15)  Get back pointer
                                   13424                       ST    R4,PCBQB-PCB(,R15)  Set back ptr to new entry
                                   13425                       STM   R15,R0,PCBQF-PCB(R4)  Set ptrs for new entry
                                   13426                       LR    R15,R0              Put ptr is reg for index
                                   13427                       ST    R4,PCBQF-PCB(,R15)  Set for ptr of prev to new
                                   13428                       AIF   ('&STCK' NE 'YES').EXIT
                                   13429                       STCK  PCBQCLCK-PCB(R4)    Save TOD when buffer put on queue

                                   13434              .*
                                   13435              .*  Dequeue the buffer in R4 from its current queues by updating

                                   13437              .*    by this entry.
                                   13438              .*

                                   13440                       L     R1,PCBQB-PCB(,R4)   Get backward entry

0                                  20303              *
                                   20304              * the following routine is used to obtain a  resource  for
                                   20305              * use.   a  resource is obtained by searching for the name
                                   20306              * of the resource type in the resource group  list.   when
                                   20307              * the  resource  type  is found the free resource queue is
                                   20308              * searched for a free resource; the free resource is taken
                                   20309              * off the free queue and queued to the active queue.   the
                                   20310              * current  JCB  is then set in the owners slot and the ECB
                                   20311              * and flags are cleared.  return is made  to  the  caller.
                                   20312              * the entry parameters are as follows:
                                   20313              *
                                   20314              *     register           contents
                                   20315              *        0                JCB addr of requestor
                                   20316              *        1                address of resource name
                                   20317              *       15                resource obtain request:
                                   20318              *
                                   20319              *  the following obtain requests are defined:
                                   20320              *
                                   20321              *       4   -   wait for the resource if unavailable
                                   20322              *       8   -   return if resource is unavailable
                                   20323              *      12   -   queue JCB & return if resource unavail
                                   20324              * upon return from the resource obtain routine the
                                   20325              * exit parameters are as follows:
                                   20326              *
                                   20327              *      register          contents
                                   20328              *         0               address of resource entry block
                                   20329              *         1               address of resource
                                   20330              *        15               return code as follows:
                                   20331              *                         0  - R0,R1 are set as above
                                   20332              *                         4  - JCB was queued
                                   20333              *                              and return was made
                                   20334              *                         8  - resources busy|attn
                                   20335              *
 001533 00/50E0 D000/902_          20336              GETRSC   XENTER TRACE=NO
 USING  *,R7

0                                  20810              *
                                   20811              * the following routine is used to return a resource  that
                                   20812              * the  current  JCB  owns.  this is done by looking up the
                                   20813              * resource name in  the  resource  group  list,  and  then
                                   20814              * looking  up  the JCB in the active resource queue.  when
                                   20815              * (if) found, the resource is  dequeued  from  the  active
                                   20816              * queue  and requeued onto the free queue.  then the queue
                                   20817              * of waiting JCBs is examined to find the first JCB on the
                                   20818              * queue waiting for the resource.  this  JCB  is  dequeued
                                   20819              * from  the  JCB queue and is assigned the freed resource.
                                   20820              * the JCB is then queued to the setup queue and return  is
                                   20821              * made  to  the  caller.   the  entry  parameters  are  as
                                   20822              * follows:
                                   20823              *
                                   20824              *    register           contents
                                   20825              *      0                 JCB address of requestor
                                   20826              *      1                 pointer to resource name
                                   20827              *
                                   20828              * upon return from the  resource  free  routine  the  exit
                                   20829              * registers are set as follows:
                                   20830              *
                                   20831              *    register     -     contents
                                   20832              *      0                 arbitrary
                                   20833              *      1                 arbitrary
                                   20834              *     2-8                same as on entry
                                   20835              *     15                 return code as follows
                                   20836              *                         0  -  resource returned ok
                                   20837              *                         4  -  JCB doesn't own resource
                                   20838              *

0                                  24237              ¿þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþÜ
                                   24238              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   24239              Ÿ  MGETNEW -- Routine to get a new "memory page" in PAR.              Ÿ
                                   24240              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   24241              Ÿ    A memory page is a WYLBUR page that is kept in virtual           Ÿ
                                   24242              Ÿ    memory, not part of WYLBUR's paging system.  Memory pages        Ÿ
                                   24243              Ÿ    are used to keep information global for all users.               Ÿ
                                   24244              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   24245              Ÿ    On exit, R15 (and cc):                                           Ÿ
                                   24246              Ÿ      0 - ok; R0 = pageno;                                           Ÿ
                                   24247              Ÿ              PAR = new page data ptr                                Ÿ
                                   24248              Ÿ      4 - no more memory; R0/PAR = zero                              Ÿ
                                   24249              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   24250              Ÿ    Historical note:                                                 Ÿ
                                   24251              Ÿ      Prior to 7/86, pagenos were halfword numbers.  Now they        Ÿ
                                   24252              Ÿ      are fullwords.  If the high-order bit is on, then the          Ÿ
                                   24253              Ÿ      "pageno" is actually just the address of a memory page.        Ÿ
                                   24254              Ÿ      If the high-order bit is off, then it is pageno of a           Ÿ
                                   24255              Ÿ      disk page.  Code that never gets memory pages can still        Ÿ
                                   24256              Ÿ      get away with saving just a halfword for a pageno, but it      Ÿ
                                   24257              Ÿ      is a bad idea.  In the future, all pagenos should be           Ÿ
                                   24258              Ÿ      considered to be fullword quantities.                          Ÿ
                                   24259              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
